## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics (homogeneous/batch reactor rate laws)
**Analysis**: The target dA_dt is a time-derivative of concentration A, which is the standard setting for ordinary-differential-equation (ODE) rate laws in chemical kinetics. With only t and A available, the most likely relationships are elementary/empirical rate laws, reversible terms, autocatalysis, inhibition, or time-varying effective rate coefficients in a batch system.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Zero-order consumption: dA_dt = -c0 (rate independent of A; e.g., surface-limited or saturated regime)
- First-order decay: dA_dt = -c0 * A (unimolecular decomposition, radioactive-like decay, pseudo-first-order kinetics)
- Second-order decay: dA_dt = -c0 * A**2 (bimolecular self-reaction, recombination)
- n-th order rate law: dA_dt = -c0 * A**c1 (empirical overall order from data)
- General production + loss: dA_dt = c0 - c1 * A (constant source with first-order removal; flow/formation plus decay)
- Reversible first-order relaxation to equilibrium: dA_dt = -c0 * (A - c1) (approach to equilibrium concentration c1)
- Autocatalytic / logistic-like kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A) (self-accelerating growth with depletion/limited capacity)
- Substrate inhibition / self-limiting consumption: dA_dt = -c0 * A / (A + c1) (rate saturates in A; effective inhibition at high A)
- Mixed-order (linear + quadratic): dA_dt = -c0 * A - c1 * A**2 (parallel first- and second-order pathways)
- Time-dependent effective first-order coefficient: dA_dt = -c0 * exp(c1 * t) * A (changing environment/catalyst activity over time)
- Power-law time modulation: dA_dt = -c0 * t**c1 * A (aging, ramped conditions, or empirical nonstationarity)
- Oscillatory forcing of rate: dA_dt = -c0 * (c1 + sin(c2 * t)) * A (periodic modulation of conditions such as illumination or feed cycling)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope Ôćĺ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects Ôćĺ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay Ôćĺ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior Ôćĺ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects Ôćĺ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Mass-action sign constraint: for consumption of A alone, dA_dt is typically non-positive and often proportional to A**n; production terms flip the sign or add offsets
- Order identification via curvature: linear dependence on A suggests first-order; strong curvature in dA_dt vs A suggests higher-order (A**2, A**c1) or mixed pathways
- Equilibrium approach: presence of a stable nonzero fixed point A = c1 is indicated by dA_dt changing sign around A - c1 (structures like -(A-c1))
- Autocatalysis signature: dA_dt increases with A at low A but decreases after a peak (often captured by A*(c1-A) or A - A**2 terms)
- Saturation/inhibition in A: diminishing sensitivity of dA_dt to A at large A suggests rational forms like A/(A+c1) or (A-c1)/(A+c2)
- Parallel pathways: if dA_dt vs A cannot be fit by a single power, additive loss terms (A + A**2) often represent concurrent mechanisms
- Time-varying conditions: systematic drift of rates over t at fixed A suggests multiplicative time factors (exp(c*t), t**c) multiplying an A-dependent core rate law
- Periodic operation/forcing: repeating patterns in residuals over t suggest sinusoidal modulation of the effective rate coefficient
- Finite-time depletion vs long tail: very rapid early drop with slower late decay can indicate higher-order kinetics transitioning effectively toward lower-order behavior or inhibition-like rational terms

============================================================

GT Equivalence Verification (CRK23)
============================================================
GT: -c0*sqrt(A) + c1*_p*sin(c2*A)
Candidate formulas: 50

GT is the fixed function (of variable **A** only):
\[
f(A)=-0.1001695596\sqrt{A}+0.4714850169\sin(0.8555148186\,A)
\]
So any matching candidate must be able (possibly under a domain restriction like \(A\ge 0\)) to produce **(i)** a \(\sqrt{A}\) term with a nonzero coefficient and **(ii)** a single sinusoid in \(A\) with adjustable amplitude/frequency/phase, and **(iii)** no extra nonzero terms (unless they can be set to 0 by parameters).

Key observation: Every candidate listed is built from combinations of \(A\), \(A^2\), rational functions in \(A\), logs/exp, \(|A|\), Max, etc., plus sine terms. **None** contains \(\sqrt{A}\) (i.e., \(A^{1/2}\)) or any construct that can be tuned to equal \(\sqrt{A}\) on a continuous domain (other than trivial single points). Conditional equivalence like ÔÇťassume \(A\ge 0\)ÔÇŁ can turn \(|A|\) into \(A\), but it cannot turn any of these building blocks into \(\sqrt{A}\).

Below I still check each candidate for whether it could possibly generate the needed \(-k\sqrt{A}\) term (it cannot), and whether the sine part could match (often yes by parameter choice), but failing the \(\sqrt{A}\) term is fatal.

---

### 1. \(A c0 + A c1 + c2\sin(A c3 + c4)\)
Only linear-in-\(A\) plus sine. No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match GT.

### 2. \(A c0 + c1\sin(A c2 + c3)\)
Linear + sine. No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 3. \(A c0 + A c1 + A c2 + c3\sin(A c4 + c5)\)
Linear + sine. No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 4. \(A c0 + A c1 + A + c2\sin(A c3 + c4)\)
Linear + sine. No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 5. \(A c0 + A c1 + A c2 + A + c3\sin(A c4 + c5)\)
Linear + sine. No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 6. \(A c0 + A c1 + c2\sin(A c3 + c4) + c5\log(c6\log(c7|A c8|+1)+1)\)
Has linear, sine, and nested logs of \(|A|\). Even with \(A\ge 0\), logs cannot equal \(\sqrt{A}\) on an interval. Cannot match.

### 7. \(A c0 + A c1 + A + c2\sin(A c3 + c4) + c5\log(c6\exp(c7\sin(A c8 + c9))+1)\)
Extra log(exp(sin)) term; cannot become \(\sqrt{A}\). Setting \(c5=0\) removes it, leaving linear+sine (still no \(\sqrt{A}\)). Cannot match.

### 8. \(A c0 + A c1 + \frac{A c2}{c3 + c4|A|^2 + |A|} + A + c5\sin(A c6 + c7)\)
Rational term in \(A\) and \(|A|\); cannot equal \(\sqrt{A}\) on a continuous domain. If \(c2=0\) it reduces to linear+sine. No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 9. \(A c0 + A + c1\sin(A c2 + c3)\)
Linear+sine. No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 10. \(A c0 + A c1 + c2\sin(A c3 + c4) + c5\log(c6\exp(c7\sin(A c8 + c9))+1)\)
Same issue as #7: either keep log term (not \(\sqrt{A}\)) or set it to 0 and still no \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 11. \(A^2 c0 + c1\sin(A c2 + c3)\)
Quadratic+sine. No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 12. \(A c0 + A c1 + 2A + c2\sin(A c3 + c4)\)
Linear+sine. No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 13. \(A c0 + A c1 + A c2 + A c3 + A c4 + c5\sin(A c6 + c7)\)
Linear+sine. No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 14. \(A c0 + A c1 + c2\sin(A c3 + c4) + c5\max(0, A + c6)\)
Piecewise linear via Max; still no \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 15. \(A^2 c0 + A c1 + A c2 + A + c3\sin(A c4 + c5)\)
Polynomial+sine. No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 16. \(A c0 + A c1 + \frac{A c2}{A^2 c3 + A + c4} + A c5 + c6\sin(A c7 + c8)\)
Rational term; cannot equal \(\sqrt{A}\) on an interval. If rational term removed, still linear+sine. Cannot match.

### 17. \(A c0 + A c1 + A c2 + A + c3\sin(A c4 + c5) + c6\exp(c7|A c8 + c9 t|)\)
Depends on \(t\) unless \(c6=0\) (or \(c7=0\) and then itÔÇÖs constant). Either way no \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 18. \(A^2 c0 + c1\sin(A c2 + c3) + c4\sin(A c5 + c6)\)
Quadratic + sum of sines. You could set one sine amplitude to 0 and match the GT sine by choosing frequency/phase, but still no \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 19. \(A c0 + A c1 + c2 e^{c3 t} + c4\sin(A c5 + c6)\)
Has \(t\)-dependent exponential unless \(c2=0\). Then linear+sine only; no \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 20. \(A c0 + A c1 + A c2 + \frac{A c3}{A c4 + 1} + A + c5\sin(A c6 + c7)\)
Rational + linear + sine. No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 21. \(A c0 + A c1 + \frac{A c2\log(c3|A|+1)}{A + c4} + A + c5\sin(A c6 + c7)\)
Log/rational term cannot become \(\sqrt{A}\) on an interval. If removed, linear+sine. No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 22. \(A c0 + A c1 + c2\sin(A c3 + c4) + c5\log(A c6 + 1)\)
Log term cannot equal \(\sqrt{A}\) on an interval; removing it leaves linear+sine. No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 23. \(A c0 + A c1 + c2\sin(A c3 + c4) + c5\sin(c6\log(c7 e^{A c8}+1)+c9)\)
Extra nonlinear sine-of-log term; can be zeroed with \(c5=0\), leaving linear+sine. No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 24. \(A c0 + A c1 + A c2 (t+1)^{c3} + A c4 + c5\sin(A c6 + c7)\)
Has \(t\) unless \(c2=0\). Then linear+sine. No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 25. \(A c0 + A c1 + A + c2\sin(A c3 + c4) + c5\sin(c6\log(c7 e^{A c8}+1)+c9)\)
Same as #23/#4: can reduce to linear+sine but no \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 26. \(A c0 + A c1 + \frac{A c2}{A c3 + 1} + A c4 + c5\sin(A c6 + c7)\)
Rational+linear+sine. No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 27. \(A c0 + A c1 + \frac{A c2}{c3\max(0,A)+1} + A c4 + c5\sin(A c6 + c7)\)
Piecewise rational; still no \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 28. \(A c0 + A c1 + A + c2\sin(A c3 + c4) + c5\log(c6\sin(c7 e^{A c8}+c9)+1)\)
Log(sin(exp)) term not \(\sqrt{A}\); can be removed but then linear+sine. No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 29. \(A c0 + A c1 + A c2 + A + A^{c3} c4 + c5\sin(A c6 + c7)\)
This has a power term \(c4 A^{c3}\). If we could set \(c3=\tfrac12\), weÔÇÖd get a \(\sqrt{A}\) term. **But** the candidate uses \(A**c3\) with free exponent \(c3\), so in principle it *can* represent \(\sqrt{A}\) by choosing \(c3=1/2\) and \(c4=-0.1001695596\). Then we must eliminate linear terms by setting \(c0=c1=c2=0\) and also remove the extra \(+A\) termÔÇöbut the standalone \(+A\) is fixed and cannot be zeroed. Therefore it cannot match GT.

### 30. \(A c0 + A c1 + A c2 + A c3|A| + A c4 + c5\sin(A c6 + c7)\)
Has \(A|A|\) (i.e., \(A^2\) for \(A\ge0\) and \(-A^2\) for \(A\le0\)), plus linear+sine. No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 31. \(A c0 + A c1 + A + c2\sin(A c3 + c4) + c5 e^{c6/(c7+t)}\sin(A c8 + c9)\)
Has fixed \(+A\) and a \(t\)-dependent amplitude unless \(c5=0\). Still no \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 32. \(A c0 + A c1 + A + c2\sin(A c3 + c4) + c5\log(A^{1/3} c6 + 1)\)
Has fixed \(+A\); log term not \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 33. \(A c0 + A c1 + A + c2\sin(A c3 + c4) + c5 e^{A c6}\)
Has fixed \(+A\); exponential term removable but still no \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 34. \(A c0 + A c1 + \frac{A c2}{A c3 e^{c4 t} + c5 e^{c4 t}} + A c6 + A + c7\sin(A c8 + c9)\)
Has fixed \(+A\) and \(t\)-dependence unless \(c2=0\) (or \(c4=0\) and still rational). No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 35. \(A c0 + A c1 + c2\sin(A c3 + c4) + c5\sin(c6\log(c7|A|+1)+c8)\)
Extra sine-of-log; can set \(c5=0\) leaving linear+sine. No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 36. \(\frac{A^2 c0}{A+c1} + A^2 + A c2 + A^{c3}c4 + A^{c5}c6 + c7\)
Has power terms \(A^{c3}\), \(A^{c5}\) so could create \(\sqrt{A}\) by setting one exponent to 1/2. But it also has an unavoidable \(+A^2\) term (fixed coefficient 1) which cannot be removed. So cannot match GT.

### 37. \(A c0 + A c1 + c2\sin(A c3 + c4) + c5 e^{c6\sin(A c7 + c8)}\)
Extra nonlinear exp(sin) term removable with \(c5=0\), leaving linear+sine. No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 38. \(A c0 + A c1 + c2\sin(A c3 + c4) + c5 e^{c6 t}|A|^{c7}\)
Could make \(|A|^{c7}\) into \(\sqrt{A}\) by choosing \(c7=1/2\) and restricting domain \(A\ge0\) so \(|A|^{1/2}=\sqrt{A}\). But the coefficient includes \(e^{c6 t}\), which depends on \(t\) unless \(c6=0\). If \(c6=0\), coefficient becomes constant \(e^0=1\), so we can set \(c5=-0.1001695596\) and get the \(-0.1001695596\sqrt{A}\) term (under \(A\ge0\)). Then we must remove linear terms by setting \(c0=c1=0\), and match the sine by setting \(c2=0.4714850169\), \(c3=0.8555148186\), and \(c4=0\) (or any \(2\pi k\)). **This would match GT perfectly under domain \(A\ge 0\)** *except* GT has no \(t\) dependence at all, and with \(c6=0\) the \(t\) dependence is gone. So this candidate **can** match GT under \(A\ge0\).

### 39. \(\frac{A^2 c0}{A+c1} + A^2 + A c2 + A^{c3}c4 + c5\)
Unavoidable \(+A^2\). Cannot match.

### 40. \(\frac{A^2 c0}{A+c1} + A c2 + A^{c3}c4 e^{A c5}\)
Even if \(A^{c3}\) gives \(\sqrt{A}\), the \(e^{A c5}\) factor must be 1 (set \(c5=0\)) to match GT; then still has rational term unless \(c0=0\). But then it becomes \(A c2 + c4 A^{c3}\), no sine term at all. Cannot match.

### 41. Big rational expression with denominator \(A+c0\)
This is a rational combination of powers; no sine, no \(\sqrt{A}\) unless via \(A^{c4}\) but still divided by \(A+c0\). Cannot match GTÔÇÖs sine term and \(\sqrt{A}\) simultaneously. Cannot match.

### 42. \(\frac{A^2 c0}{A^2+c1} + A c2 + A c3 + A c4 + A + c5\sin(A c6 + c7)\)
Unavoidable \(+A\). No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 43. \(A c0 + A c1 + A + c2 e^{c3 t} + c4\sin(A c5 + c6)\)
Unavoidable \(+A\). Cannot match.

### 44. \(A c0 + A + A^{c1}c2 e^{A c3} + \frac{A^{c4}c5}{A^{c4}+c6}\)
Unavoidable \(+A\). Also no plain sine. Cannot match.

### 45. \(A c0 + A c1 + A c2 + \frac{A^{c3}c4 e^{c5 t}}{c6\max(0,A)^{c3}+1} + c7\sin(A c8 + c9)\)
The fraction term is complicated and \(t\)-dependent unless \(c4=0\). If \(c4=0\), left with linear+sine only (no \(\sqrt{A}\)). Cannot match.

### 46. \(A c0 + A c1 + \frac{A c2}{A+c3} + c4\sin(A c5 + c6)\)
Rational+linear+sine. No \(\sqrt{A}\). Cannot match.

### 47. \(A^2 c0 + A c1 + c2 + c3 e^{c4\sin(A c5 + c6 t + c7)}\)
Has \(t\) inside sine unless \(c6=0\), but still no \(\sqrt{A}\) and no way to get it. Cannot match.

### 48. \(A^{1/3}c0 e^{A c1} + A c2 + c3 e^{A c4} + c5 e^{c6 t}\sin(A c7 + c8)\)
Has \(A^{1/3}\), exponentials; cannot become \(\sqrt{A}\) term. Also sine amplitude \(t\)-dependent unless \(c6=0\). Cannot match.

### 49. \(A^{1/3}c0 e^{A c1} + A c2 + A + c3 + c4 e^{A c5}\log(c6 t + 1) + c7/A^5\)
Unavoidable \(+A\) and other terms; no sine. Cannot match.

### 50. \(A c0 + \frac{A c1}{A+c2} + A + A^{c3}c4 e^{A c5} + \frac{A^{c6}c7}{A^{c6}+c8}\)
Unavoidable \(+A\); no sine. Cannot match.

---

Only candidate **38** can reproduce both required components (\(\sqrt{A}\) and \(\sin(kA)\)) with parameters, under the plausible domain restriction \(A\ge 0\).

Concrete matching choice for #38:
- Domain: \(A\ge 0\)
- Set \(c0=0,\; c1=0\)
- Sine: \(c2=0.47148501687516587,\; c3=0.8555148185506902,\; c4=0\)
- Root term: \(c6=0\) (so \(e^{c6 t}=1\)), \(c7=\tfrac12\), \(c5=-0.10016955960092372\)

Then candidate 38 becomes:
\[
-0.1001695596\,A^{1/2}+0.4714850169\sin(0.8555148186\,A)
\]
which equals GT for \(A\ge 0\).

GT Equivalence Verification (CRK23)
============================================================
GT: -c0*sqrt(A) + c1*_p*sin(c2*A)
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: [29, 45]
Matched candidates: ["A*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2 + A + A**c3*c4 + c5*sin(A*c6 + c7)", "A*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2 + A**c3*c4*exp(c5*t)/(c6*Max(0, A)**c3 + 1) + c7*sin(A*c8 + c9)"]

I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the Ground Truth:

**GT: -0.10016955960092372*sqrt(A) + 0.47148501687516587*sin(0.8555148185506902*A)**

The GT consists of two basis functions: `sqrt(A)` and `sin(c*A)`.

Let me analyze each candidate to see if it can match this form.

**Key observation:** The GT has `sqrt(A)` and `sin(linear in A)`. Most candidates have terms like `A*c` (linear in A) and `sin(A*c + c)`. A linear function of A is NOT equivalent to `sqrt(A)` - these are linearly independent basis functions. So any candidate that only has polynomial terms in A plus sin terms cannot match unless it also contains `sqrt(A)` or `A^(1/2)` or equivalent.

Let me check each candidate:

**Candidates 1-5, 9, 12-13:** These have `A*c` (linear terms) + `sin(A*c + c)`. Linear in A Ôëá sqrt(A). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 6:** Has `A*c + sin + log(c*log(c*|A| + 1) + 1)`. The log-log term cannot produce sqrt(A). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 7, 10:** Has `A*c + sin + log(c*exp(c*sin(...)) + 1)`. Cannot produce sqrt(A). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 8:** Has `A*c/(c + c*|A|^2 + |A|)` - rational function of A, not sqrt(A). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 11:** `A┬▓*c0 + c1*sin(A*c2 + c3)`. A┬▓ Ôëá sqrt(A). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 14:** Has `Max(0, A + c)`. For A Ôëą 0 and c=0, this is A. Still linear. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 15:** `A┬▓*c0 + A*c + sin`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidates 16, 20, 26, 27, 46:** Have rational functions of A like `A*c/(A*c + 1)`. These are rational, not sqrt. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 17, 19, 24, 31, 34, 38, 43, 45, 47, 48:** Contain `exp` or `t` terms. Setting exp coefficients to 0 leaves polynomial + sin, which can't match sqrt(A). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 29:** Has `A^c3 * c4`. If c3 = 0.5, this gives `c4*sqrt(A)`. Combined with sin term: `A*(c0+c1+c2+1) + c4*sqrt(A) + c5*sin(A*c6+c7)`. Set c0+c1+c2+1=0, then we get `c4*sqrt(A) + c5*sin(A*c6+c7)`. **MATCH!**

**Candidate 30:** Has `A*c3*|A|` = `c3*A┬▓` for AÔëą0. No sqrt. **NO MATCH**

**Candidates 32, 33:** log(A^(1/3)*c + 1) or exp(A*c) - not sqrt. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 35:** `sin(c*log(c*|A|+1))` - not sqrt. **NO MATCH**

**Candidates 36, 39, 40, 41, 42, 44, 49, 50:** These have `A^c` terms. Let me check:
- **36:** `A^c3*c4 + A^c5*c6` - could set c3=0.5, but also has A┬▓ terms that can't be zeroed (explicit `A**2`). **NO MATCH**
- **39:** `A^c3*c4` with c3=0.5 gives sqrt, but no sin term. **NO MATCH**
- **40:** No sin term. **NO MATCH**
- **41:** Has `A^c4` terms but no sin. **NO MATCH**
- **44:** `A^c1*c2*exp(A*c3)` + `A^c4*c5/(A^c4+c6)`. No sin. **NO MATCH**
- **Candidate 50:** No sin. **NO MATCH**
- **Candidate 23, 25, 28, 37:** Complex compositions, no sqrt source. **NO MATCH**
- **Candidate 22:** log(A*c+1) Ôëá sqrt(A). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 45:** Has `A^c3*c4*exp(c5*t)/(...)`. Setting c5=0 gives constant*A^c3, with c3=0.5 Ôćĺ sqrt(A). But also Max(0,A)^c3 in denominator. With c6=0, denominator=1. Then: `A*(c0+c1+c2) + c4*A^0.5 + c7*sin(A*c8+c9)`. Set linear=0. **MATCH!**
